# Early Medieval (501-1000 CE)

*1025 Mibera birthdays from this era.*

---

## 11/12/502 Ce 04:27

**Mibera(s):** [#1285](../miberas/1285.md)

**Era:** Early Medieval (502 CE)

*Dark Ages in West. Islamic Golden Age begins. Tang Dynasty flourishes.*

---

### Astrological Snapshot

**Sun Sign:** Scorpio

- **Element:** Water
- **Modality:** Fixed
- **Ruler:** Pluto/Mars
- **Traits:** intense, transformative, mysterious, powerful

*death and rebirth, shadow work, psychic depths*

**Time of Birth:** 04:27 (Pre Dawn)

*Liminal hour between worlds. The veil thins.*

*Peak solar power. Maximum visibility and vitality.*
